#Medicina statica, or, Rules of health in eight sections of aphorisms / originally written by Sanctorius ... ; English'd by J.D.#

##Santorio, Santorio, 1561-1636.##

##Content Summary##

#####Front#####
Medicina Statica: OR, RULES OF Health, In Eight Sections OF APHORISMS. Originally written by SanctorThe Weighing Chaira man sitting in a chair on a pulley system, with a meal on a table in front of hiLICENSED,May 23. 1676.Roger L'Eſtrange.
1. TO THE Much Honour'd, W. WitheringsEſq.

1. Sanctorius TO THE READER.

1. An Account of the Weighing Chair.

1. THE SECTIONS.

#####Body#####

1. The Firſt Section.
